          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3309535-nonie-serenity2bliss?shelf=favourite">favourite</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2645484965" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2478825304635498126">I was wary to read this because the plot and the title screams Mills & Boon to me and that is not a good thing.<br/><br/>But much to my surprise, it was anything but like M&B. <br/><br/>It was a fun, sweet, sexy read. Think of it like a modern day Cinderella story but with hurricane and sans glass slippers. It didn't take me more than a day to 'feast' on this sexy sucker. <br/><br/>I like Bronte a lot. Her wits and quips are charming. I like that she is no damsel in distress.<br/><br/>I love Logan. I like that he is cold but he doesn'</span>
  <span id="freeText2478825304635498126" style="display:none">I was wary to read this because the plot and the title screams Mills &amp; Boon to me and that is not a good thing.<br><br>But much to my surprise, it was anything but like M&amp;B. <br><br>It was a fun, sweet, sexy read. Think of it like a modern day Cinderella story but with hurricane and sans glass slippers. It didn't take me more than a day to 'feast' on this sexy sucker. <br><br>I like Bronte a lot. Her wits and quips are charming. I like that she is no damsel in distress.<br><br>I love Logan. I like that he is cold but he doesn't come across as arrogant. Dull, maybe. Hot, yes yes yes! <br><br>I don't know why I have never give Jessica Clare any notice but she got my attention now!<br><br>Highly recommended for those who are looking for a satisfying sweet romance that is not over the top (except maybe for the whole billionaire secret society with secret language stuff).<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504828773ra/23828575.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1299415149" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1299415149" />
    <a title="Lover of Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance"><img alt="Lover of Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1458253423p2/3709091.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1299415149?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lover of Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lover of Romance" href="/user/show/3709091-lover-of-romance">Lover of Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3709091-lover-of-romance?shelf=genre-contemporary">genre-contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1299415149" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4099869760568930666">Summary <br/>Bronte, was thrilled when she won a trip to a Bahama resort, but her luck turns when a hurricane comes in, and during the chaos she is stuck in a elevator with a man she believes to be the manager of the resort. After some time, they realize that no one is coming for them, and they must rescue themselves. They manage to get out of the elevator, and find the resort abandoned, both Bronte and Logan forgotten. They spend days together, and a connection forms, passion erupts and they spend t</span>
  <span id="freeText4099869760568930666" style="display:none">Summary <br />Bronte, was thrilled when she won a trip to a Bahama resort, but her luck turns when a hurricane comes in, and during the chaos she is stuck in a elevator with a man she believes to be the manager of the resort. After some time, they realize that no one is coming for them, and they must rescue themselves. They manage to get out of the elevator, and find the resort abandoned, both Bronte and Logan forgotten. They spend days together, and a connection forms, passion erupts and they spend those precious days together learning each other, but then Bronte learns when they are rescued who Logan really is, a Billionaire that became the resorts newest owner. And before Bronte realizes it she is thrown into a world that is so unknown to her, a world that she isn’t sure she can fit into to, but will the love Bronte and Logan have be enough to last?<br /><br />The Hero <br />Logan, is a billionaire, and is part of a brotherhood that became close friends in college and they made a pact with each other. A pact that must remain secret at all costs. Logan, doesn’t know love or affection. All he knows is the greed of women, and how they just see him for his credit card and not as a real person. He has little faith in women until he meets Bronte who charms him with her knowledge of Plato and is so honest and genuine that he can’t resist her. What was truly fun about Logan as the hero, is that he is a man that wants something real in a relationship. You see how he needs it and isn’t afraid to admit it or when he is wrong. He is much deeper than a rich businessman, we see how much he needs love and a woman that will stand up to him.<br /><br />The Heroine <br />Bronte, is a heroine that you just admire, and she sparks some interest in ancient history. Bronte has a degree in ancient history, but still works as a waitress because despite the horrid pay, she loves working with people. She is carefree and down to earth, and loves the simple things in life. What was most fun about Bronte as a character was seeing how she handles conflict and challenge. She is quite brave and she maintains her own identity when brought into Logan’s world of prestige and wealth.<br /><br />Plot and Story Line <br />I have been hearing some great things about this series, so I decided to read the first book up, and boy did I love this story. It just kept me so interested and involved, and the authors writing is superb…I love the way she makes the reader fall in love with the story. I am not always a big fan of billionaire romances, they have to be done right, and despite my reservations, I fell for this story hard. I loved everything about it. From the island fling that Logan and Bronte have, to making love in a freezer, how Bronte wins over his friends, and the way she gets Logan to become humble…and even the signs of another love story that is in the next book. What was most fun about this story was seeing how Logan and Bronte flounded their way through a relationship, both side makes mistakes but I found that most endearing…seeing them make mistakes but still find a way to work as a team and make a future together. There was many aspects of their relationship that was easy to relate with in a very realistic way. From beginning to end, I found myself falling in love with this story…with its charm and poignant love story…its guaranteed to warm your heart.<br /><br />The Cover <br />I honestly don’t know what I think about this one. In all honest I like it, I don’t mind a little bling-bling, but what my issue is how it relates with the story. I do prefer something that connects better with the story and characters. So as of right now I am undecided if I love it or not.<br /><br />Overall View <br />Stranded With A Billionaire is a charming love story that shows how love tests us all in ways we don’t quite imagine. This is a love story that promotes passion and raw emotion, and learning to trust again. Heartwarming from beginning to end!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4099869760568930666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_578568258" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578568258" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578568258?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578568258" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13872314542315524753"><b>4.5 Fairytale Stars</b><br/><br/>If you are looking for a cute read that has a damsel in distress story line with a sexy billionaire, then this is your book. I love my crazy reads, but every once in a while, I want a no fuss, no mess, oh-my-gosh, it’s too adorable, please- rescue-me kind of book.<br/><br/><b>Summary</b><br/><br/>Logan is part of a society of men who are all wealthy (yeah, it’s kind of cheesy because they call themselves a “brotherhood”, when it should be just a club, but just go with it). All his life, people have used</span>
  <span id="freeText13872314542315524753" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Fairytale Stars</b><br><br>If you are looking for a cute read that has a damsel in distress story line with a sexy billionaire, then this is your book. I love my crazy reads, but every once in a while, I want a no fuss, no mess, oh-my-gosh, it’s too adorable, please- rescue-me kind of book.<br><br><b>Summary</b><br><br>Logan is part of a society of men who are all wealthy (yeah, it’s kind of cheesy because they call themselves a “brotherhood”, when it should be just a club, but just go with it). All his life, people have used him because he is rich and because of that he is guarded and doesn’t do relationships.<br><br>Bronte is a waitress and wins a beach vacation. She’s poor and has a college degree but is very content in life. Since a storm is approaching the beach, everyone is being evacuated, but Bronte is stuck in the elevator with sexy Logan, who she doesn’t know owns the resort.<br><br><b>Review</b><br><br>Not the whole book is written Bronte and Logan stuck on the island, but a good chunk of it is (about 30%). I really liked the beginning because it’s just too CUTE! Bronte doesn’t know who Logan is, she thinks he’s a manager and so she kind of complains about the resort and what needs to be done to make it better. Logan doesn’t want to say anything because he is enjoying Bronte’s company because she is treating him like a normal person.<br><br>The attraction is pretty there and being the only two people left on the island, it’s pretty easy for the two to have insta-lust. Stranded with a Billionaire is very steamy. <br><br>I really liked the relationship between Logan and Bronte. I liked that Bronte doesn’t care about money and is shocked by the gifts Logan tries to give her. Logan is kind of a brute and isn’t too nice to Bronte, but he does care for her, so he tries.<br><br>I can understand the ratings, the story line isn’t overly dramatic, but sometimes I like that! I like the whole, falling in love with a Billionaire, but not knowing he’s rich story line. I read this in one sitting and I will keep up with the series. <br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17561022.Stranded_with_a_Billionaire__Billionaire_Boys_Club___1_" title="Stranded with a Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #1) by Jessica Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1362603720s/17561022.jpg" alt="Stranded with a Billionaire (Billionaire Boys Club, #1) by Jessica Clare" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/0425269078/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=0425269078&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=ZZR6HLDFKQSQJPZQ" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13872314542315524753" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer5037104967685269241">Perfect (most horrible) vacation checklist<br/><br/>Win vacation on radio station CHECK<br/>Find annoyingly worst most self absorbed companion possible CHECK<br/>Make sure a hurricane is about to arrive CHECK<br/>Find yourself stranded with a stranger and have your own blue lagoon moment CHECK<br/><br/>Bronte Dawson doesn't live above her means, she is a sock hop waitress who won a dream vacation, which has quickly turned into a livable nightmare. She ends up stranded in the middle of the hurricane with a complete stranger, Logan</span>
  <span id="freeText5037104967685269241" style="display:none">Perfect (most horrible) vacation checklist<br /><br />Win vacation on radio station CHECK<br />Find annoyingly worst most self absorbed companion possible CHECK<br />Make sure a hurricane is about to arrive CHECK<br />Find yourself stranded with a stranger and have your own blue lagoon moment CHECK<br /><br />Bronte Dawson doesn't live above her means, she is a sock hop waitress who won a dream vacation, which has quickly turned into a livable nightmare. She ends up stranded in the middle of the hurricane with a complete stranger, Logan Hawkings. Bronte thinks Logan is the manager of the hotel and finds a comfort in the uptight intense man.<br /><br />Logan is used to being used by women, he is a billionaire and he is so tired of the fake behavior of women just looking for a one way ticket to his pocket book. Realizing that Bronte has no clue who he is, he finds himself giving in to the pull of the quirky waitress who quotes ancient philosophy. There intimate island experience quickly implodes though when Bronte finds out who he really is. Logan is willing to fight for Bronte, but he is not used to dealing with a woman who holds her own and wants nothing from him other than just being himself.<br /><br /><br />Loved, loved, loved if I was caught in a hurricane, please give me Logan. He is curt to all others but to Bronte he softens into this incredible man who is just trying to win Bronte's heart. Need an escape, this is the book for you.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SlGsMMvk6lmAXH/8li7YXGFErWQzPEvRNWi1m60CYZewOrqdWvt0G26+GD8/Q+NGR9wicRF2wnmgHky3IanTkg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EoBOSyYOJDyhxt3tP4CSLvMtn9HzcvAtpG1E/XXjbzLo61jmtxG6fk8kui6W7ak01bUQxNE4eYUxG73R+UjdNw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer14141856034518421280">This is a pen name for <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2923539.Jill_Myles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jill Myles</a>.<br/><br/>Jill Myles has been an incurable romantic since childhood. She reads all the 'naughty parts' of books first, looks for a dirty joke in just about everything, and thinks to this day that the Little House on the Prairie books should have been steamier.<br/><br/>After devouring hundreds of paperback romances, mythology books, and archaeological tomes, she decided to write a fe</span>
  <span id="freeText14141856034518421280" style="display:none">This is a pen name for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2923539.Jill_Myles" rel="nofollow noopener">Jill Myles</a>.<br /><br />Jill Myles has been an incurable romantic since childhood. She reads all the 'naughty parts' of books first, looks for a dirty joke in just about everything, and thinks to this day that the Little House on the Prairie books should have been steamier.<br /><br />After devouring hundreds of paperback romances, mythology books, and archaeological tomes, she decided to write a few books of her own - stories with a wild adventure, sharp banter, and lots of super-sexy situations. She prefers her heroes alpha and half-dressed, her heroines witty, and she loves nothing more than watching them overcome adversity to fall into bed together.</span>
